<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:smeer.html>smeer</a> (3717)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:smeer.html>smeer</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">smero</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*smerwą</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">smear</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

***smelten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:smelten.html>smelten</a> (7145)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:smelten.html>smelten</a></i>, a merger of two <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> verbs:
</p>
<ul><li><i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*smeltan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*smeltaną</i>, a strong intransitive verb.</li>
<li><i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:smelten.html>smelten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*smaltijaną</i>, weak causative of the above.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smelten.html>smelten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to melt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boter.html>boter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gesmolten.html>gesmolten</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The butter <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <b>molten</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to melt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boter.html>boter</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gesmolten.html>gesmolten</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I have <b>molten</b> the butter.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:smelten.html>smelten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paashaas.html>paashaas</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They are <b>melting</b> the <a href = vnd.unilang:easter.html>Easter</a> bunny!</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:smeren.html>smeren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*smirwen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*smirwijaną</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*smerwą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grease, fat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smeer.html>smeer</a></i>).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:smidse.html>smidse</a> (72863)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">smitse</i>, reformed from earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">smisse</i> by analogy with <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">smit</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smid.html>smid</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*smiththa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*smiþjǭ</i>. The development *-þj- gt; -ss- <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also found in <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wisse.html>wisse</a></i>, while *-þþ- becomes -tt- in <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lat.html>lat</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mot.html>mot</a></i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">smiten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*smītan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*smītaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*smeyd-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">smieten</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">smite</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schmeißen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">smite</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">smide</i>.

***smoren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:smoren.html>smoren</a> (23685)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smoren.html>smoren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to smother, to suffocate, to deprive of oxygen</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to muffle, to repress, to diminish, to <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive, intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to braise</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to smoke weed</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:smoren.html>smoren</a></b>
</p>

***smous.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:smous.html>smous</a> (50695)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">משה</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">moyshe</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Moses</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, pronounced <i>moushe</i> in Western Yiddish, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">מֹשֶׁה</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">moshé</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Moses</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smous.html>smous</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smous.html>smousen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">smouzen</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smous.html>smousje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ethnic slur<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">Jew</span> <span class="defdate">[from mid 17th c.]</span></li>
<li>A small breed of terrier with a light to dark <a href = vnd.unilang:beige.html>beige</a> fur, native to the Netherlands. <span class="defdate">[from mid 19th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1848</b> May 11, Advertisement 7018, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:algemeen.html>Algemeen</a> Handelsblad</i>, No. 5136, page 4.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vermist.html>Vermist</a> :</b> Den 9den <a href = vnd.unilang:mei.html>Mei</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kleine.html>Kleine</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jonge.html>Jonge</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>Hond</a>,</b> Poesbaard of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:smous.html>Smousje</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:kleur.html>kleur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lichtbruin.html>Lichtbruin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> eenig <a href = vnd.unilang:zwart.html>Zwart</a> doorgeslagen, <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hals.html>hals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderste.html>onderste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedeelte.html>gedeelte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vier.html>vier</a> pooten <a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a>,<a href = vnd.unilang:luisterende.html>luisterende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:naam.html>naam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <b>DJALMA.</b></span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">MISSING: The 9th of <a href = vnd.unilang:mai.html>Mai</a>, one SMALL YOUNG DOG, "Cat beard" or <b>little <a href = vnd.unilang:smous.html>Smous</a></b> (indication of breed), color: Light Brown with some Black coming through, the front of the neck and the down part of the four <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a> White, listens to the name DJALMA.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">smoushond</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:snacken.html>snacken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*snakkon</i>. ***sneeuwbal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sneeuwbal.html>sneeuwbal</a> (24043)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sneeuw.html>sneeuw</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">snow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ball</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sneeuwbal.html>sneeuwbal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sneeuwballen.html>sneeuwballen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sneeuwbal.html>sneeuwballetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

***sneeuwen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sneeuwen.html>sneeuwen</a> (15899)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sneuwen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:sneeuwen.html>sneeuwen</a></i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sneeuw.html>sneeuw</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>. Displaced Middle Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">snuwen</i> due to analogy with <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:regenen.html>regenen</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hagelen.html>hagelen</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sneeuwen.html>sneeuwen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to snow</li></ol>

</p>
